(Tokyo) The Research Group and other factions of the House of Peers are very indignant at the current situation where the Diet has been delayed in deliberation due to the Seiyukai's proposed bomb-like motion, and the atmosphere of supporting the government has become stronger, becoming a state of exciting the government. The House of Peers' General Budget Committee opened at 9:40 a.m. yesterday. Baron Okura Kimmochi of the Koseikai questioned Prime Minister Okada on the Manchurian immigration issue, and then pressed the Prime Minister to express concrete aspirations regarding the national policy of Manchuria. The Prime Minister replied that not only will the independence of Manchukuo be supported and preserved, but also various forms of cooperation will be implemented to achieve coexistence and co-prosperity. Okura asked how Minister of the Army, as Director-General of the Manchurian Affairs Board, is fully responsible for Manchurian affairs in general. Is the activities of the Manchurian Affairs Board a transferring or decision-making mechanism? Are all Manchurian affairs carried out by the Affairs Board? What is the relationship between the Affairs Board and other government departments? Regarding the Kwantung Governor-General, who has full power in Manchuria, and the Kwantung Army, which has the higher authority? Is there no confusion? Why must active-duty soldiers be placed under the Kwantung Governor-General? Is the Kwantung Army's Special Affairs Department abolished, or is there a similarly transformed mechanism? What is the reason for the Army Chief of Staff serving concurrently as the Director-General of Affairs? Minister of the Army Hayashi replied that the first point is to closely respect the independence of Manchukuo and the inseparable relationship between Japan and Manchuria. Director-General of the Legislative Bureau Kanamori replied that the Affairs Board is a supplementary mechanism to the Prime Minister and does not directly exercise its will. Those that should be unified from the viewpoint of the national policy toward Manchuria are carried out by this mechanism. The matters managed by the Kwantung Governor-General and the Commander of the Kwantung Army are different, so there is no confusion. Appointing the Commander of the Gendarmerie to be the Chief of the Police Department is not to turn the Gendarmerie into police, but to unify police affairs. Okura asked that it is regrettable that the Kwantung Governor-General participates in general industry and economic matters. The Prime Minister replied that I intend to entrust him with industrial and economic matters in a broad sense. Minister of the Army Hayashi replied that the official system has not yet been announced. I mean that the Kwantung Governor-General cannot handle the affairs of Manchukuo. Okura finally stated his hope that the official system would be decided according to his intention. Russia and France Sign New Agreement 52

(Geneva) French Foreign Minister Laval and Soviet Russian Foreign Affairs Commissar Litvinov agreed that during the negotiations on the Eastern European Mutual Assistance Pact, neither party would enter into any "bilateral agreements." This ambition remains unchanged." Litvinov continued, stating that both Russia and France view the Eastern European Mutual Assistance Pact as a necessary factor in stabilizing European peace, and the two governments are determined to continue their efforts to achieve it. This can also be seen in the recent agreement signed by the two countries. The threat of disrupting peace still exists. Although the authorities of a certain country have issued unilateral declarations, claiming to cherish peace, the threat of disrupting peace has not been eliminated because of this. Moreover, in addition to this peace declaration, there are also declarations of the opposite nature. Therefore, to eliminate the threat, it is necessary to establish objective, definite, and material guarantees. The Franco-Russian agreement was signed on the 5th of this month, and there is still the possibility of signing other agreements in the future. This agreement does not restrict France and Russia from continuing to sign other agreements in the future. However, no matter what agreement, its purpose is definitely not against a third country, but in the case of being invaded, it cannot be generalized. If other countries can join this agreement, the mutual relations between the signatory countries will be no different from the regular relations between France and Russia. I deeply believe this. Soviet Russia has always hoped to establish the best possible relations with Germany. If the Eastern European Mutual Assistance Pact can be established, good relations can be established between France, Germany, Russia, and other signatory countries, and the international political situation can be comforted and stabilized as a result. This is what Europeans desire. Various measures are currently being taken internationally, and the sole spirit is to maintain peace. For example, the resolution of the Saar issue is one aspect of this. The agreement signed between Russia and France echoes this kind of measure," and so on. (Havas Dispatch, 7th)

Heated Debate Between Representatives of Yugoslavia and Hungary at the League of Nations Council Meeting 53

Yugoslav Foreign Minister Accuses Hungary of Being Responsible for the Marseille Incident

Says This Action Has No Political Effect in Maintaining Peace

Hungarian Representative Refutes, Insisting on Revising the Peace Treaty

France and the Little Entente Countries Clearly Show Support for Yugoslavia

(Geneva) The League of Nations Council met at 3 PM yesterday to discuss the dispute between Yugoslavia and Hungary. The chairman, Portuguese representative Vasconcellos, reported the start of the meeting, and then Yugoslav Foreign Minister Yeftich stood up and read a declaration in a peaceful and firm tone, largely restating the memorandum previously submitted to the League of Nations. He said that Yugoslavia had to accuse Hungary of being responsible for the Marseille assassination in order to maintain peace. The Yugoslav government did this because terrorist parties are rampant in Hungary and have become a raging fire. Yugoslavia believes that responsibility lies where it should and that there is no turning back. Having said this, the Yugoslav Foreign Minister reiterated the evidence cited in his memorandum one by one, and finally solemnly declared that this action by the Yugoslav government has no political effect whatsoever, but only seeks a legal judgment. After the Yugoslav Foreign Minister finished his speech, Hungarian representative Eckhardt stood up to respond, taking about 45 minutes, refuting each point made by the Yugoslav Foreign Minister, and recognizing it as a planned movement by Yugoslavia to slander Hungary for several weeks. (National Telegram, 8th)

(Geneva) The League of Nations Council held a meeting, the first to discuss the Yugoslav application. No unexpected events occurred at the meeting. Most of the foreign representatives and journalists were present. The chairman of the Council, Portuguese representative Vasconcellos, first read Article 11 of the League of Nations Covenant, which stated in its second section that any situation affecting international relations that could disrupt international peace or the good understanding on which international peace depends, any member of the League has the right to bring to the attention of the Assembly or the Council. The chairman then invited Yugoslav Foreign Minister Yeftich to speak. Yeftich rose and delivered a speech, saying that the Yugoslav application revealed the responsibility of the Hungarian administrative organs and government for the Marseille incident. Its purpose was to maintain peace and had no political effect whatsoever. Yeftich stated the reasons according to the application, and strongly stated that Hungary should be held responsible. Yeftich said that Yugoslavia is also willing to expand the scope of discussion to establish an international agreement to punish terrorism. Hungarian representative Eckhardt denied all the events revealed by Yugoslavia, saying that the Marseille assassination was not prepared in Hungary. The late King Alexander of Yugoslavia was put to death by revolutionaries, and the revolutionaries were active outside of Hungary. Eckhardt also said that the peace treaty created a kind of revolutionary situation, and the Marseille tragedy was its manifestation. Eckhardt then said that only by revising the peace treaty can peace in Central Europe be maintained and international cooperation be achieved. The Hungarian representative also refuted the accusations of the Little Entente countries, saying that it was a political means and asked the League of Nations Council to investigate. (Note: After the Yugoslav government submitted an application to the League of Nations on November 22, the Czech and Romanian governments also sent official documents to the League of Nations separately to express their sympathy to Yugoslavia.) After Eckhardt finished his speech, Romanian Foreign Minister Titulescu stood up to answer, saying that since Eckhardt regarded the official documents sent by the Little Entente countries to the League of Nations as a political means, then the Hungarian reply to the Yugoslav application (Note: The Hungarian reply was postponed to the 8th after gentle persuasion from Britain and Italy) must be submitted for public discussion and refuted, otherwise this debate cannot be concluded. Chairman Vasconcellos then said that after the Hungarian reply is submitted, all related countries can reply on Monday. Turkish Foreign Minister Rüştü said that before taking common measures internationally, all related countries should take necessary sanctions to stop terrorism. Czech Foreign Minister Beneš then took the floor to explain the reasons why Czechoslovakia fully agreed with the Yugoslav application. He said that Czechoslovakia's intention was nothing more than to use the power of the Council to eliminate the current conflict and prevent it from happening again. Beneš also said that for some time, some people have been plotting to endanger the integrity and security of Czechoslovakia on the northern border of Hungary, and the situation is the same as what the Yugoslav application said. The newly created countries of Central Europe are striving for unification, which has been the case since ancient times, and conspirators want to prevent the trend of unification among countries. If someone wants to destroy the unification of Yugoslavia, Czechoslovakia, or Romania, it will lead to an inevitable disaster. "I specifically declare this important point," and so on. Beneš's remarks clearly indicate that the League of Nations has the function of pacifying incidents. The next meeting is scheduled to be held at 3 PM tomorrow. (Havas Dispatch, 7th)

Situation of the League of Nations Council Meeting Yesterday 54

(Geneva) The League of Nations Council held an open meeting. French Foreign Minister Laval expressed his opinion, saying that the accusations made by the Yugoslav government against Hungary were shocking. Schools and Hospitals Temporarily Provide Shelter

Yugoslavia's Actions Will Lose International Sympathy

The boundary line between Yugoslavia and Hungary is only a small dry ditch, but the peace treaty signed by the two countries calls it a waterway. According to a dispatch from Reuters correspondent in Budapest, the number of Hungarian nationals expelled from Yugoslavia and who have arrived in Hungary to date is 2,436. Many more are waiting to be transported to the border by car. It is now believed that all 30,000 Hungarian nationals in Yugoslavia will be expelled. Serbians now despise Hungarians more and more, and it is expected that the border will be closed in a few days. (Reuters Dispatch, 7th)

Organization of International Troops to Maintain Saar Security Begins 56

Total of Five Battalions, Britain and Italy Each Contribute Two

British Officer to Serve as Commander-in-Chief

Switzerland Does Not Participate, Netherlands Has Not Yet Replied

(Geneva) The subcommittee composed of British General Temperley, Italian General Visconti, League of Nations Secretary-General Avenol, and Saar Region Administrative Committee Chairman Knox held a meeting this morning to discuss various proposals regarding the dispatch of troops to the Saar, so that they could be submitted for discussion at the closed-door meeting of the Council at noon. It is said that the international troops will total about 5,000 personnel, under the command of a British officer. Sweden and the Netherlands have not yet given a definite reply on whether to participate. On the contrary, the Swiss Federal Administrative Committee, after receiving a semi-official invitation, has expressed its unwillingness to participate, on the grounds that Switzerland does not have standing troops that can be sent abroad. At its noon meeting, the League of Nations Council decided to expand the Saar three-person committee (namely, Italy's Alessio, Argentina's Gandilo, and Spain's Madariaga) so that each country sending troops could send one representative to join as a military expert. These international troops will consist of five battalions, including two British battalions, two Italian battalions, and one battalion jointly sent by the Netherlands and Sweden. They will enter the Saar before Christmas this year (December 25). After the expansion of the three major committees, they will be responsible for drafting the organizational details of these international troops and submitting proposals to the Council. (Havas Dispatch, 8th)

The Hague, The Dutch government learned today that the League of Nations is about to ask it to send some police to join the international troops sent to the Saar to maintain order during the plebiscite. The other participants will be Britain, Italy, and Switzerland. (Reuters Dispatch, 7th)

Litvinov Speaks on the Saar Issue 57

(Geneva) At the League of Nations Council meeting, the report of the Third Committee on the Saar issue was discussed. Litvinov said, "The so-called Saar issue is most relevant to the two major nationalities, has less impact on the signatories of the Treaty of Versailles, and as for other countries such as the Soviet Union, this issue is only related to being a member of the League of Nations. Its responsibility is only for the resolution of general peace issues and the effects after its implementation. From this point of view, we do not need to explain why we fully agree with the suggestions made by the Third Committee (based on the agreement of the two countries concerned). However, there are several issues that must be taken into account by all members of the Council. These issues relate to the fate of the Saar people, which is still in the hands of the League of Nations Council. Fortunately, the Saar people will soon be able to decide their own fate. At that time, we will process their decisions made in a free and unhindered plebiscite. The right to self-determination that we speak of often refers to the right of the people of a certain place to join any country or establish their own government. If the Saar people have such possibilities, then we believe that any decision they make will be the final decision, and at the same time, the Council does not need to worry too much about their fate. Unfortunately, this case has a special feature, that is, its decision can be called unprecedented in international practice, and the theory of international law has not seen it before. Specifically, the Saar people can not only merge with any of their neighboring countries, but also continue their existing regime. This change of power is obviously temporary. We firmly believe that this decision is only adopted temporarily for special reasons, so it is no wonder that the various groups in the Saar and individuals participating in the plebiscite have repeatedly inquired with the Council and certain committees about the legal importance of this decision. At the same time, they inquired whether this decision is final in nature. In other words, after this decision is passed, will the Saar people permanently lose their right to self-determination? It is not surprising that the committee had to answer these questions. The committee has determined that if the result of the plebiscite is in favor of maintaining the existing system, then the Saar governance will be transferred to the League of Nations. At that time, the League of Nations will be able to use this governance to slightly change the legal status of the Saar. If the most relevant countries do not interfere in the slightest, then the Saar people also eagerly hope that the League of Nations' maintenance of power should have no other purpose than to safeguard the peace of the League of Nations. Therefore, in the future, if the Saar people clearly express their willingness to change their legal status, then the League of Nations must not deny their right to self-determination unless it uses the reason that they could not use their right to self-determination before." Litvinov then recalled the solemn declaration made by the foreign minister of one of the countries most concerned about this issue, who said that his country would never interfere with this position of the League of Nations. Litvinov then said, "If another major country concerned with this issue can come to this occasion again (this is what I eagerly hope for), will it raise objections? I dare to assert that it will not. In this arena, I believe that the other member states of the League of Nations will never reject the legitimate request of the Saar people to make a revised decision for temporary reasons." Litvinov continued, "I have no suggestions. What I said is only to explain why I agree with the opinions put forward in the committee report. These opinions are consistent with the principle of self-determination and my interpretation, so I do not object to this report. I hope that the passage of this report will be able to meet the wishes and interests of the Saar people and all parties concerned, and will be able to promote world peace." (TASS Dispatch, 7th)

(Washington) The famous novelist H.G. Wells recently published the second volume of his autobiography, in which he described his meeting with former President Hoover in the US Presidential Palace, saying that President Hoover was "overworked, resulting in a state of weakness and incompetence." Now, former Hoover Secretary Lee has made a correction, saying that Wells' book is fictitious and close to insulting, and that Wells was never allowed to meet, and had never entered the White House, because Hoover did not grant a meeting. Later, at the strong request of the British Embassy, Hoover hastily met Wells in his office for no more than two minutes. Now he uses this hasty meeting to write a book, falsely claiming that President Hoover is weak and incompetent, and that routine official matters are mostly piled up for a month. It is not known what he is basing his claims on. He also said that the White House is messy and disorganized, which is also out of fantasy, because during Hoover's tenure, he never set foot in the White House. As for the statement that his visit was presumptuous, this is the only truth. (National Telegram, 7th)

The London gold price today was quoted at 140 shillings and 8 pence, up 4 and a half pence.

There was not much change in the silver market futures at Mountrie.

The British and American London foreign exchange market was very quiet this morning. The opening exchange rate between the British and American currencies was 4 yuan, 9 jiao, 4 fen, 1875, which was 3125 lower than yesterday's closing exchange rate. The popularity of the pound sterling later turned slightly stronger, and the closing price was 4 yuan, 9 jiao, 4 fen, 6875, which was half a cent higher than the opening price.

The opening price of British and French currencies was 75 francs, and then rose by three pounds to 75 francs and 03. This price did not change until the close.

In the American and British New York foreign exchange market, the pound sterling opened slightly stronger, with a price of 4 yuan, 9 jiao, 4 fen, 625, which was 125 higher than yesterday. It then fell back 125 to 4 yuan, 9 jiao, 4 fen and a half. This is the latest price.

The average number of private forecasts for cotton production in New York this morning was 9.6 million bales, but the government estimates may be slightly higher. The cotton market opened at a price two pounds higher. Since there was no pressure from sellers, and the industry also bought in slightly, the price continued to rise slightly.

Current U.S. Economic Situation (U.S. Correspondence) 95

Mutual Trade Development

Increase in Farmers' Income

Republicans spare no effort to attack President Roosevelt's new policies, but for more than a year, they have not seen any special effects. However, the United States assumes that if it does not implement the N.R.A. policy and does not convert to a new policy, there is no other better way to change the general economic decline in the United States today. However, one point worth noting is that after 1930, all countries in the world implemented protectionist trade policies and increased tariffs, resulting in a tariff war. The higher the tariff barriers, the smaller the foreign market, and the domestic market does not necessarily have room for development. After suffering this lesson, the United States deeply knows that this policy cannot be fundamentally changed, and it is not enough to change the current congested state of world trade.

Therefore, the United States is preparing to reduce tariffs and implement mutual benefit agreements. The first country to conclude a mutual benefit agreement with the United States was Cuba. The implementation of the mutual benefit agreement began on September 3 this year. According to the calculation at the end of September, the total amount of Cuban sugar imported into the United States from January to August this year was only 73 million pounds, while in September alone, it was 153 million pounds. This is truly an amazing miracle. The US exports to Cuba have also increased significantly. For example, the exports of wheat flour to Cuba last September were worth 197,000 US dollars, and this September increased to 298,000 US dollars. Cotton yarn was worth 3,800 US dollars last September, and this year it increased to 16,000 US dollars. Pork lard was only worth 38,000 US dollars last September, and this year it increased to 298,000 US dollars in the same period. Cured meat also increased from 23,000 US dollars last year to 93,000 US dollars this year. Looking at Cuba alone, this number is certainly very small, but for the entire US trade, the value of exports in September was 196.69 million US dollars, and the value of imports was 131.659 million US dollars. The export surplus was 65.031 million US dollars. Although the number is not very large, it is the largest export surplus since 1931. It is the result of implementing mutual benefit agreements and reducing tariffs. In the future, mutual benefit agreements will be discussed with South American countries, Belgium, Spain, etc.

This autumn, the domestic economy is still in a state of stagnation. The industrial production index has continued to fall since May. In September, it was the lowest record since March last year. The working capacity of the steel industry was only 18.4% of the total production capacity in early September, and by October it had not fully recovered to 26.3% of the total capacity. Compared with the figure of 57.4% of the total production capacity reached in June this year, it is less than one-half. The biggest reason for the decline of the textile industry is that 400,000 workers were on strike for more than three weeks. In September, the average weekly production of cotton was only 70 million square yards, which is also less than half of the first half of the year. Other industries such as cement industry, automobile industry, etc. are lower than last year.

Since industrial production has declined, the situation of workers will inevitably worsen. According to the survey of the American Federation of Labor, the number of unemployed people in September was 10,951,000, which is 11,700 more than in August, and 843,000 more than the 10,108,000 in September last year. The increased number cannot be said to be small, and the economic future cannot be said to be stable.

However, on the other hand, there is a strange phenomenon, that is, this autumn, retail sales in various department stores are very good. Whether it is the index of department store expenditures investigated by the Federal Reserve, they have maintained very high figures in August and September. Why do department stores have such good sales during the industrial recession? One is that the wage reduction in various industrial sectors is very small, and all those who are employed retain their original purchasing power. The second is due to the drought. Agricultural products are restricted by nature, and market prices rise, so the purchasing power of farmers is slightly higher. The third is that the government spends a huge amount of drought relief funds. With this subsidy, the rural economy is more active. According to the economic report of the Agricultural Adjustment Administration, the purchasing power of farmers in August this year increased by 44% compared with March last year. However, this optimistic material is ultimately lacking in permanence. Even if the general society is stimulated by the "New Deal" and shows some lively scenes, if the industry cannot be revitalized, the future hope is still not great. It can only be seen after the implementation of the mutual benefit tariff agreement, or there may be a turnaround in the international community. (October 29 in New York)

Transfer of Hebei Provincial Government to Baoding May Not Be Realized Before the New Year 96

Baoding Lacks Sufficient Housing

Joint Office to be Implemented on New Year's Day

Tianjin Correspondence, The relocation of the Hebei Provincial Government to Baoding has been rumored for a long time. Initially, because the officials were tight-lipped, the public could not know the details. It was not until the Executive Yuan passed the case a few days ago that the officials allowed it to be announced. However, Provincial Government Secretary-General Wei Jian said yesterday that the central government's order had not yet reached the province. The provincial government has been moved from Bao to Tianjin for a long time. Once it moves back to Baoding, there will be many difficulties, such as the lack of large houses suitable for joint offices. Even the former Cao Family Garden of the old provincial government has been abandoned for many years and is dilapidated. If it is repaired, it will take a considerable amount of time. It is feared that it will not be possible to move there before the solar new year, or even before the lunar new year. There are rumors that the provincial government has sent people to Bao to repair the houses, but that is not the case. Since the Hebei provincial capital was moved from Tianjin, all undertakings have been declining. Now that there is news that the provincial government will move there, the society has suddenly become active. Major stores and banks in Tianjin and Ping have gone to inspect the location and expand their business, and the prices of houses in Baoding have increased.

According to Yu Xuezhong's intention, the joint office of the provincial government will be realized on January 1 next year. After the joint office, the organizational law of the provincial government and various departments will be drafted with reference to the current example of Hubei Province and the special circumstances of this province. The provincial government will set up a secretariat with four sections under it. The first section will be in charge of receiving and sending, general affairs, and accounting. The second section will be in charge of personnel and transfer. The third section will be in charge of statistics and auditing. The fourth section will be in charge of inspection and examination. In addition, a security office will be set up to unify the security teams in the war zones of the province, the Hebei Provincial Security Team, the newly編 Special Police Team, the county defense groups, and the police public security teams. The four departments of civil affairs, finance, education, and construction were originally four-section systems. After the joint office, the first section will handle general affairs, which will be under the charge of the first section of the provincial government secretariat. Each department will only have three sections, and the number of personnel will be reduced by about one-third compared with the present. Because the province is implementing the abolition of exorbitant taxes, which is limited to the end of the year, the only way to compensate for the insufficient funds is to start with reducing government expenditures, so the joint office is also taking the opportunity to save on payments. The old provincial government houses in Baoding are smaller than the current Tianjin provincial government. In the future, when moving to Bao, the various departments will have to merge a part in order to realize the joint office.

Before the provincial government moves to Baoding, it plans to first eradicate the banditry in the province. This was decided at the 589th routine meeting of the provincial government on the 4th of this month. Elite troops will be selected from the 51st Army to suppress the bandits in separate routes. Currently, the most rampant banditry in the province is in Yongqing and Gu'an, secondly in Wuqiang and Suning, and thirdly in Xinhe. Among them, Xu Erhei's gang in Yongqing, with about 300 people, has been wreaking havoc in the surrounding counties. The provincial government believes that although the bandits are rampant, they can be easily wiped out by the formal army. The logistics supply is being properly planned by the provincial government. Once the 51st Army selects the troops, they will be dispatched separately. (6th)

Financial Disturbance in Chaozhou and Shantou 97

Shanghai Cash Cannot Be Transported to Chaozhou and Shantou Anymore

Credit Crunch Creates Stagnation in Various Industries

Authorities Issue Announcements Strictly Prohibiting Disturbances to Travelers

Shantou Correspondence, Chaozhou and Shantou have been experiencing industrial and commercial decline, rural desolation, a credit crunch, a rise in foreign exchange, and an increasingly chaotic financial market in recent years. The Department of Finance approved merchants and citizens to issue commercial treasury certificates of 10 million yuan based on real estate for relief. However, when the issuance was approaching 4 million yuan, a fake treasury certificate scandal occurred. The credit of the treasury certificates and the original guaranteed banknotes was lost at the same time. In order to consolidate their credit, most silver firms transported cash from Shanghai to Shantou. Since October, the amount of cash imported has been no less than 3 million yuan. The silver industry association and its member silver firms formed a mutual aid association to exchange banknotes on a daily basis, preparing to exchange the banknotes for commercial treasury certificates for use in order to achieve uniformity. Currently, the soft currency circulating in Shantou City includes guaranteed banknotes, circulating coupons, auxiliary coins, and white tickets. According to the Department of Finance's order, they must all be exchanged for commercial treasury certificates within the specified period. White tickets are gradually being recalled, and the amount is about 1.2 million yuan. Other guaranteed currencies are being registered. The new commercial treasury certificates are being printed by the Xinhua Company in Hong Kong and are divided into four types: 100 yuan, 50 yuan, 30 yuan, and 20 yuan, each with 2.5 million yuan. If the new certificates are printed and issued, the old certificates must be cancelled, and various banknotes can no longer be used in the city. During this transition period, the financial market is chaotic, with no standard price. Exchanging banknotes for cash requires a surcharge of 11 yuan per 100 yuan. There are four types of banknote prices: the Provincial Bank's silver dollar coupons are the highest, the banknotes of reputable silver firms are the second highest, the banknotes of non-convertible silver firms are the third highest, and the circulating coupons issued by the Chamber of Commerce after being closed are the lowest. Commercial treasury certificates and white tickets have a face value of 100 yuan per sheet, and the price changes several times from morning to night. It is difficult to use currency in Shantou, and there are losses in both collection and change. The Eastern District Office, upon the request of the Chamber of Commerce, announced that people are not allowed to refuse to accept soft currency or create disturbances when exchanging it, and violators will be punished as disrupting financial order. However, soft currency can only be used in the Shantou urban area and cannot circulate in the counties and villages. Every winter solstice, when soil sugar is on the market, sugar merchants need cash to purchase soil sugar from the villages. In addition, overseas Chinese in Southeast Asia send remittances back to their hometowns, which are particularly numerous at this time, exceeding 3 million yuan per month. Overseas Chinese remittance agencies also need cash to distribute remittance silver to the villages.

Page 10

Chaozhou and Shantou have always been import-surplus ports. Merchants handle a considerable amount of goods in winter, and the amount remitted to Hong Kong to repay debts each month is no less than 10 million yuan. Remittances also require cash. When cash is scarce, the Hong Kong-Shantou exchange rate is particularly high, requiring a surcharge of 380 yuan per 1,000 yuan of Hong Kong paper, which is unprecedented. According to the exchange rate, bringing cash to Hong Kong can yield a net profit of more than 180 yuan to 200 yuan per 1,000 yuan. Therefore, the smuggling of cash for export is increasing, and the cash on the market is becoming increasingly scarce. The means by which unscrupulous merchants transport silver for export are quite clever, either melting it into silver blocks, or casting it into gold bars, or hiring young children to take a small amount of cash on board in shifts and hide it in secluded places. All kinds of tricks are used. The customs and police discover the matter of gold and silver being smuggled every day, with an average of more than 10,000 yuan per day. However, legitimate travelers are suffering from harassment. The Department of Finance issued an announcement stating that each person is only allowed to carry 20 yuan of silver and must not exceed the limit. However, some merchants and travelers who carry more than ten yuan for travel expenses, or even only a few yuan, are also searched. Ordinary travelers are in tears, complaining everywhere. For example, in the market towns of coastal counties, local products such as pigs, cattle, vegetables, and green fruits are usually transported to Shantou for sale. However, after selling them, cash cannot be taken out. If remittances or delivery methods are used, there is no cash available in the counties. The Chamber of Commerce of Lufeng County specially requested the Shantou authorities to allow merchants and citizens of the county to carry cash back to the county, but the authorities did not approve it, because it is very convenient for fishing boats to travel between Lufeng and Hong Kong, and they are afraid that cash will flow out of the country. Shantou Chen Bingchun and other silver firms felt that there was an urgent need for cash on the market, so they handled 1.2 million yuan of cash in Shanghai, preparing to transport it to Shantou, but it was stopped by the Ministry of Finance and could not be transported. The Exchange Association and the Overseas Chinese Remittance Association sent telegrams to Shanghai requesting its release, but it is said that they were all ineffective. According to merchants, the reason why the Ministry of Finance does not allow cash to be transported to Shantou and Xiamen is that last month, Shantou silver merchants distributed 400,000 yuan to Shantou, but later they calculated that it would be profitable to transport it to Hong Kong, so they did not unload it in Shantou. The Ministry of Finance believes that merchants only have this plan, so they resolutely stopped transporting silver south. Currently, the only way for the Chaozhou and Shantou authorities to relieve the financial situation is to carry out searches for smuggling, even if travelers complain and the countryside is desolate, they do not care. However, the Department of Finance recently issued an announcement to Shantou, stating that Huang Xiuting's letter stated that smuggling of silver for export by unscrupulous merchants should be strictly prohibited, but customs officials and police are taking the opportunity to make a fortune, taking all the proceeds of the search into their own pockets, and even ignorant women and children who do not understand the prohibition, or pass through the coastal areas of Hong Kong and Macao, must take all their belongings with them.

However, once they enter the dock or get on a small boat, regardless of whether they are smuggling, they will confiscate all their silver coins, and even the 20 yuan that is allowed to be carried will not be given. This kind of lawless robbery is more serious than the smuggling of silver by unscrupulous merchants, and those who are robbed occur every day. There are also repeated reports in the newspapers, but it has not been heard that the government has taken any measures to stop it. Therefore, the disturbances at the fire ship docks have been rampant in recent days, with customs officials and police colluding with each other, and merchants and travelers are uneasy and public opinion is boiling. If this continues, what kind of world will it be? Ting witnessed and heard it with his own eyes, and he could not bear it any longer, so he had to submit his complaint, requesting that the aftermath be handled well, etc. The order prohibiting the export of silver has been announced by this Department many times, and it is on record that each person must not carry more than 20 yuan. Those who are within 20 yuan are of course allowed to carry it freely. Now it is said that customs officials and police are taking the opportunity to harass them in the name of inspection, and even the 20 yuan in cash that is allowed to be exported within the limit is being confiscated. If this is true, it is very inappropriate and should be strictly prohibited to reassure merchants and travelers. This announcement has already arrived in Shantou, but it is not known what its effect will be.

Northwest Inspection Notes

— Special Correspondent Geng Ya

Limitless Joy 98

On the morning of the fifteenth, the Korean Consort's cavalry bid farewell and returned. A small gift of tea was presented, along with a letter of gratitude, entrusted to them for delivery to Commander Ma. Shiban Jing (Stone Slab Well) is a waist station with sweet, cool well water. From the former mountains, one retreats southeast, while the northwest offers a vast, flat expanse. About five or six hundred miles away, a long, wide curve can be faintly seen, its silver light sparkling, floating high in the sky. If it were said to be clouds, it lacks the light, floating appearance. If it were said to be mountains, the surrounding area is all azure sky. This is the Tianshan (Heavenly Mountains) snow peaks that traverse Xinjiang, dividing the province into two.

The Tianshan mountain range originates from the Kokshal Tau Mountains between Xinjiang and Central Asia, running east between the Ili and Weigan Rivers, where it is called Khan Tengri Mountain. Passing Dihua, it is called Bogda Mountain, and ends east of Hami, called "West Mountain" and "East Mountain". The entire range is highest at Khan Tengri (translated as King of the Heavenly Mountains), reaching 21,000 feet. The south side of the mountains is called the Southern Route of the Tianshan, and the north side is called the Northern Route of the Tianshan. In the past, when Zuo Zongtang entered Xinjiang, he passed through here and once exclaimed, "Feeling happily as if returning to my hometown." Now, gazing at it from hundreds of miles away, one cannot help but feel boundless joy.

Setting off at noon, one looks around at the sand dunes, towering and stretching endlessly. The journey follows a dry sand river westward, with the Tianshan Mountains intermittently appearing, as if half-buried beneath the horizon. The red sun shines brightly, and white clouds swirl around the mountainside like a jade belt. The terrain gradually slopes downwards, quite different from the direct ascent to Xingxing Gorge from Anxi. However, it is still referred to as "up." (Coming west from Lanzhou is called "up," and vice versa is called "down." Travelers coming and going greet each other the same way, never asking about the safety of Gansu or Xinjiang. They always ask about "dou jia," how high or how low the price is. This is because Gansu Province suffers from frequent droughts, and Xinjiang is also experiencing crop failures this year. The travelers' anxiety about food is understandable. After forty li, one reaches Shaquan Jing (Sand Spring Well), where a spring emerges from the sand dunes, as thick as the mouth of a bowl. A ditch leads the water to the roadside, forming a pool. The ditch's edge is covered with "yan ye" (small grass). The sound of the spring is clearly audible, and two wild ducks are swimming in the pool. The platoon leader first shoots one of them. The remaining duck soars into the sky for a moment, then lands again by the pool. Another shot misses, and it flies back down as before. The crowd figures that the Gobi Desert lacks pools of water, so the duck must not want to fly elsewhere. Several people are positioned to ambush the pool's edge. When the duck lands for the third time, they fire, and it is captured. The two ducks fall down, one after the other. The platoon leader rushes over to butcher them, reciting a few scriptures during the butchering. This is because the Hui people believe in Islam and do not eat animals that are not slaughtered and contain blood. The platoon leader then uses small stones to tell fortunes, saying that three soldiers were sent out this morning to hunt wild animals. According to the divination, they can obtain one thing. If it is not a wild horse, it must be a yellow sheep. Later, the three soldiers returned empty-handed.

Shaquan Jing was originally a large station, but the shops have been completely destroyed. Only two postmen live there, and their lives are quite difficult. At the stations east of Malian Jing, the postmen's monthly salaries increase yearly, with a minimum of twenty-five yuan per month, and as much as forty or fifty yuan. If they work for nearly twenty years, they can receive a pension of one thousand yuan. This kind of treatment is roughly the same in the provinces within the Guan (passes). West of Xingxing Gorge, the postmen at each station receive 300 taels of Xinjiang silver notes per month. Half of this is used to buy iron shoes for the riding donkeys needed for their work. The remaining 150 taels, calculated at 400 taels per silver yuan, is only equal to 3 jiao, 7 fen, and 5 li. They dig cynomorium (a type of parasitic plant) to fill their bellies. Sometimes, the Hami authorities provide a few catties of white flour, barely enough to survive. It is known that the postal routes in Xinjiang in recent years are difficult to traverse, unlike the smooth roads in the interior. This is likely not entirely due to the influence of local politics, but rather the postal service itself has a shortage of income, insufficient to cover expenses, which affects the work. This is a major reason. The postal service within the Guan is developed, with a surplus in income and expenditure each year. If the surplus could be used to help the deficient, and given strong support, each additional county or station that is opened would bring more practical benefits to that county or station. Whether the frontier's transportation will develop in the future depends on this. The authorities should not ignore this. Traveling forty li west from Shuiquan Jing is Yaodianzi (Waist Shop), also known as Geda Jing (Lump Well). The well is three feet square and seven or eight feet deep, lined with wooden boards, and the water is still potable. There are ruined house foundations nearby, presumably the remains of the old shop. Wild, dry reeds grow sparsely, difficult to provide enough food for camels. At night, we ate "shou zhua fan" (hand-grabbed rice), stewed with wild duck and mutton. The duck tasted fresh, but the mutton, slaughtered in Anxi more than ten days ago, had already developed a strange odor. The shopkeeper still frequently served me the fattest pieces. I could not swallow them, so I passed them to others, who said, "Thank you for the reward." Fearing that I would be put in a difficult position again, I secretly told the Han cook, "zhua guo zhe" (the one who grabs the pot), to secretly do me a favor from now on, whether it was rice or noodles, and not to put meat in my bowl. He laughed and replied, "We people are not used to eating meat, but love to eat vegetables, and are often laughed at as livestock, only knowing how to eat grass. You, sir, are originally a distinguished guest, but unexpectedly you also cannot eat meat, and you are fighting for our cause. What to do? Although, if you want to refuse meat, it is best to pretend to have a toothache, so as not to have the shopkeeper see it and blame us for treating the guests slowly." I agreed to his suggestion, and suddenly remembered that when I left Shanghai, Mr. Tang Binhua had given me the parting words "Congratulations on going to Xinjiang to eat horse meat." Now I know that the Kazakh (similar to the Hui people, but actually different) people indeed have this custom, namely, inviting guests to choose a horse first. If the guest points to a certain horse and says "good," then it is killed for the feast. The rest is seasoned with five flavors and stuffed into the original horse's intestines, called horse sausage, especially considered a precious gift for guests. Now I have a plan to pretend to have a toothache, so that when I really encounter horse meat, I will have a way to deal with it.

That day's journey covered eighty li, along sandy wastes that stretched as far as the eye could see. There were slight mounds and hillocks, but they did not obstruct the flat, open expanse. Grasslands were scarce, but the weather felt gradually warmer.

A Record of the Actual Survey of the Guiding-Huai River Project 99

A report from Zhenjiang: The Guiding-Huai River Project is divided into two routes: one into the Yangtze River and the other into the sea. The river route is being carried out by the Central Guiding-Huai River Committee, starting with the construction of ship locks. The sea route is being managed by the Jiangsu Provincial Government, and the groundbreaking ceremony was held on November 1st in Yangzhuang, Huaiyin, by Chairman Chen Guofu himself. On the first of this month, this reporter followed the special vessel of the He Zhishi, Mamao, and Jia River Works Bureau north to conduct an on-site survey. The details are recorded as follows:

We set sail at 8:00 AM that day and arrived in Shaobo at 11:00 AM to visit the Shaobo ship lock project. This project is one of the three locks in the Central Guiding-Huai River Committee's plan to channel water into the Yangtze River. The first section is in Liu Lao Jian on the Grand Canal, the second is in Huaiyin, and the third is this lock. The three locks are largely the same: 100 meters long and 10 meters wide, with a lock chamber that can accommodate fifteen 30-ton ships, six 80-ton or 100-ton ships, four 300-ton ships, or one 900-ton ship. Once the three locks are completed, the water depth from Sanjiangyingkou on the Yangtze River along the Grand Canal to the Grand Canal Station, where it intersects with the Longhai Railway, a total of 350 kilometers, will be at least three meters (about one zhang in the old Chinese measurement). Ships with a draft of 2.5 meters and a load capacity of 900 tons can navigate year-round without obstruction. Both ends of the lock chamber, upstream and downstream, have two steel lock gates. The sides and bottom of the gates are all cast in reinforced concrete. The sloping sides inside the lock, connected to the bottom, are all inlaid with stone blocks. There are water pipes placed on both sides of the lock chamber bottom, connecting the upper and lower lock gates, and equipped with opening and closing mechanisms. On top of the walls on both sides of the lock gates, for ships coming from upstream, water must first be released into the lock through the water pipes to make the water level in the lock chamber equal to the upstream level, and then the upper lock gate is opened (the opening and closing mechanisms can be operated by the strength of four people), and the ship smoothly enters the lock. At the same time, ships waiting to go upstream in the chamber can exit the lock. Then the upper lock gate is closed again, and the water is discharged downstream through the water pipes, so that the water inside the chamber is equal to the downstream level, and then the lower lock gate is opened. The downstream ship in the chamber can then exit the lock and sail downstream, while the upstream ship can enter the lock, and the lower lock gate is closed again, repeating the cycle. Each entry and exit takes at most one hour. The maximum difference in water level between upstream and downstream is 7 meters and 7 cun. Each lock costs approximately 500,000 yuan and is expected to be completed in April next year. It is being undertaken by the Fu Ji Construction Company. Most of the materials are foreign goods. The project office is in Fanxing Temple in Hexi. Director Lei Xiaofeng has gone to Beijing, and Engineer Wu Qingfan is hosting the visit. The foundations of the two lock gates are currently being driven with wooden piles, and steel sheet piles are being driven outside the wooden piles.

At 12:00, we proceeded upstream again, arriving at Gaoyou at 6:00 PM. The next morning (the 2nd), at 7:00 AM, we accompanied Zhang Weiming, the county magistrate of Taixian, Cao Boquan, the county magistrate of Gaoyou, and Messrs. Gu Zifang and Ma Shuangang. At 3:00 PM, we passed Baoying, and Mr. Qiao Mengqian boarded the ship to join us. Xu Jiecheng, the director of the Guiding-Huai River Sea Route Project Office, arrived from Yangzhou by car, abandoning the car and boarding the boat. At 5:00 PM, we passed Huaian, and Deputy Director Chen Hefu, arrived by car from Qingjiang to welcome us, also boarding the boat to travel with us. At 7:00 PM, we arrived in Qingjiang, where Chief Engineer Ge Hanlou greeted us at the pier and we stayed overnight at the project office. The next morning (the 3rd), at 8:00 AM, Mr. Xu Ge and about 20 others who had come with him, took cars to the Gaotai section of Lianshui territory to conduct an on-site survey. The cold weather here arrived early, with a north wind like a knife, and the temperature dropped below thirty degrees. Solid ice was already visible. The cars traveled on the abandoned Yellow River embankment, the distance between the two embankments being about one li at the narrowest and beyond sight at the widest. The river channel had become low-lying land. Occasional river ponds had become stagnant water. The sandy plain was endless. Looking out into the center of the river, workers were scattered among them, working. At 11:00 AM, we arrived south of Lianshui County, and rested briefly at the Gaotai section project office. According to Chief Engineer Ge, the digging is planned to be 35 meters wide and 12 meters deep. The first year's plan is to dig half the width and depth first, so that the water does not flow through. In case of a major flood next year, this half width can also be used to discharge water, and then the other half can be opened, without affecting next year's project. Every 25 workers form a group, and each group opens about 10 meters of river channel, with measurements taken every seven days, measuring the four sides of the excavation and the soil piles in the trench. The excavated soil is carried to both banks, about 200 meters, and used as a new embankment. Workers provide their own tools and work. The depth of the work varies, with some reaching three or four meters. The soil is mostly sand, so it is not difficult to dig, but it is more difficult in the ponds. The accents of Taixian and Gaoxian are completely those of farmers, and each has its own unique melody. The Taigao sections are 14.831 kilometers long in total. Lianshui is the boundary between the two counties. The project office pays wages at a rate of eight fen per cubic meter. Each person carries about one cubic meter per day, which is not enough to feed themselves, so in fact each county must subsidize it to more than one jiao per cubic meter. Assuming that each cubic meter costs a total of 1.5 jiao, then each person can earn a little extra by carrying 1.5 cubic meters per day, to prepare for food during rainy and snowy days when work is stopped. However, it is extremely difficult for each county to raise funds. Adding taxes to the fields is also hindered by orders, and if it is not taken from the fields, then industry and commerce cannot afford it. This is the biggest problem for the future of the project. At 5:00 PM, we returned to Huaiyin. The next morning (the 4th), we took a boat to visit the Huaiyin ship lock. There were originally four locks here. The downstream lock is in the north of the city, called Dazha (Great Lock). The upstream three locks are in the northwest of the city, called Fuxing (Revival), Tongji (Universal Relief), and Huiji (Beneficial Relief). The upstream three locks are very close to each other. The original intention of the ancients in building the locks was to open and close them up and down to ease the water flow and adjust the water level, the same effect as today's ship locks, except that they lacked water pipes. However, over time, the upper and lower lock gates no longer open and close, and the water still rushes through the lock. Ships going upstream must be hauled three times, and ships going downstream are unstable unless moored. As a result, the lock workers demand money. Each ship passing through the four locks costs dozens of yuan at most, and the river winds around a large bay, adding 30 miles to the journey, hindering the shipping on the Grand Canal. The current ship lock, then, is to open another diversion canal east of the three locks to take a straighter course, passing through in just over one kilometer. During the visit, we were hosted by Engineer Yin Chengzhi. The plan, in addition to the upstream and downstream lock gates having a water flow limit of 9 meters, is the same as the Shaobo lock. After this lock is completed, the old lock will be closed but not blocked, for use in flood discharge during major floods. The next morning (the 5th), we went to Huaicheng to meet with local figures to discuss issues of providing relief and conscripting labor. In the afternoon, the project office invited the county magistrates of the eight counties of Si, Huai, Lian, Huai, Bao, Gao, Tai, and Jiang, and the twelve section chiefs to a joint meeting. At the end of the meeting, Han and Ma were again invited to the table for talks, and a vote was taken on more than 30 proposals concerning conscripting labor, transportation, food, management, and sanitation. In the evening, Huaiyin County Magistrate Qi Yunlong hosted a dinner at the People's Education Hall. Messrs. Han and Ma delivered speeches during the dinner, and the evening ended on a joyous note. We returned south on the 6th and arrived in Zhenjiang on the 7th (the 8th).

Songjiang

Preparations for Winter Defense in the First District 100

As the winter season approaches, the First District of this county is proceeding with winter defense in accordance with past practice. On the 7th, it convened the township and town chiefs under its jurisdiction, and also sent a letter requesting that Section Chief Yu Shifang of the Public Security Bureau attend. Presided over by District Chief Li Zufu, it was resolved to name the office the First District Winter Defense Branch Office. The district public office is designated as the general office, and the urban and suburban areas are organized according to police districts in accordance with past practice. Yu Kuisun, Wang Yunshi, Sun Shaochi, Che Yiru, Huang Runhan, Du Lianhua, Du Yayan, Wu Juchi, Zhu Jiuwang, Xu Chunbo, and Jiang Jingcheng of Huayang District were appointed as the chief and deputy directors. It was decided that the plan would be implemented starting on the 16th of this month. Each district will recruit its own patrolmen and raise its own funds. However, the hat badges will be issued and used by the general office. The items have been reported to the county government for record.

False Alarm during a Boat Inspection in Shengzi Temple Town 101

Shengzi Temple in Punan is under the jurisdiction of the Seventh District and is the boundary between Songjiang and Fengxian. However, nine-tenths of the town market belong to Songjiang territory, and only one-tenth belong to Fengxian territory. Therefore, the Second Public Security Bureau of this county dispatched a patrol leader to set up a lookout post there. Recently, however, a platoon leader from the Third Company of the Thirteenth Security Brigade dispatched by Fengxian led three patrolmen to set up an inspection station, specializing in inspecting ships. A Songting gasoline ship passed by a few days ago, and the platoon leader ordered it to stop for inspection. The ship argued that the waters were turbulent and the boat was unable to stop immediately. Moreover, the pier belonged to Songjiang territory, but the platoon would not allow it to dock. Thereupon, they fired a shot into the air, causing panic among the townspeople. As a result, the people of the town reported to the District Chief of the Seventh District and the Second Public Security Bureau, requesting that they be stopped. After reporting to the county government, it was instructed to handle the matter to maintain the safety of travelers and the stability of the commercial market.

Ringleaders of Riot Case Escorted to Zhenjiang 102

In the villages and townships of Xietang, Luxiang, and Jiaozhi in the Suzhou countryside, riots have broken out again due to the reporting of false wastelands. An order was received instructing them to be escorted to the province for investigation. County Magistrate Wu, upon receiving the order, dispatched a platoon of security team members to escort Chen Qiutao and the six others to Zhenjiang yesterday and send them to the garrison command for interrogation.

Details of the Tragedy in Likou Township 103

The report yesterday covered the case of the robbery and theft at the home of You Caifa in Youjiabang, Likou Township, where the 63-year-old woman You Gu was hacked to death by the thieves. It is now known that You Caifa worked in Shanghai pulling a night soil cart. Only his wife Yao and his elderly mother Gu lived in the house. The night before, You Yao, due to physical fatigue, went to sleep early. Her aunt You Gu was still working at night. Around midnight, You Yao felt someone removing her earrings while she was asleep. She woke up in shock and saw her aunt You Gu lying in a pool of blood in front of the bed. She felt for her pulse, but she was already breathless. She also saw a hole in the wall, but no thieves. You Yao immediately cried for help, and neighbors rushed over upon hearing the sound. They helped in the pursuit, but the thieves had disappeared. Upon inspection, it was found that about one hundred silver dollars and gold jewelry were missing. The local headman reported to the local prosecutor's office, which sent personnel to examine the scene yesterday (the 8th). The examination confirmed that You Gu died from three knife wounds. The office ordered that a coffin be prepared for burial and notified the Public Security Bureau to strictly investigate the criminals and bring them to justice.

Wuxi

Green Poison Pill Manufacturing Den Cracked 104

Tang Baotong, a native of Changshu, was originally a medicine merchant specializing in the production of pills and powders. Seeing that selling poison pills was very profitable, he prepared a set of poison pill manufacturing machines and rented a house at No. 54 Taiping Lane in this county to privately produce green poison pills for sale in the Changshu area. Around 8:00 PM the night before last, the Inspection Department of the Public Security Bureau received a tip-off. They immediately dispatched police to the address, arrested the suspect Tang, and seized 500 green poison pills and a machine. Tang's daughter, Guiying, was also taken to the bureau and sent to the county for interrogation. Moreover, the county government received an order from the province yesterday, stating that the smuggling of private soil and highly toxic substances often involved collusion with railway employees who provided protection and used the railway for private transport. The order instructed them to strictly prevent such activities to facilitate the enforcement of prohibition policies.

Preparations to Establish a Cooperative Agricultural Warehouse 105

The County Agricultural Warehouse Management Committee of this county held its second meeting the day before yesterday afternoon. Chairman Magistrate Yan (1) reported on the provincial government's approval for the agency agricultural warehouse to collect interest and a handling fee of 1.6%. (2) Reported that the budget had been approved, limited to 50 yuan per month. (3) Reported that the fifth agency agricultural warehouse, Shengde pawnshop in Yanqiao, had sent a letter requesting to cease operations, which had been approved. (4) Reported that the Shanghai Bank Qingyang Warehouse had set up three branch warehouses in Sitoubei, Xizhang, etc. in Wuxi. (5) Reported that the Dongzhou Township Dongzhou Lane Credit and Concurrent Unlimited Cooperative Society in the Second District, and the Dazhaqiao Credit and Concurrent Unlimited Cooperative Society in Xicang Town, had applied for registration and the establishment of a cooperative agricultural warehouse, and had been forwarded to the provincial office for instructions.
